#Symbol
mendelejew_21_scandium_custom_symbol_type = {
	type = country
	random_valid = no #Choses the first valid loc from top to bottom

	text = {
		fallback = yes # If nothing else triggers, it will default to this, ignoring triggers.
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_game_rule = mendelejew_historical_element_only_names_rule
				has_global_variable = custom_element_21_scandium_global_var
			}
		}
		localization_key = element_sc
	}
	text = {
		trigger = {
			has_global_variable = custom_element_21_europium_global_var
		}
		localization_key = element_eu
	}
	text = {
		trigger = {
			has_global_variable = custom_element_21_rhenium_global_var
		}
		localization_key = element_re
	}
	text = {
		
		trigger = {
			has_global_variable = custom_element_21_polonium_global_var
		}
		localization_key = element_po
	}
	text = {
		trigger = {
			has_global_variable = custom_element_21_coppernicum_global_var
		}
		localization_key = element_cn
	}
	text = {
		trigger = {
			has_global_variable = custom_element_21_londinium_global_var
		}
		localization_key = element_ld
	}
	text = {
		trigger = {
			has_global_variable = custom_element_21_cantabrigium_global_var
		}
		localization_key = element_cb
	}
	text = {

#Symbol
mendelejew_72_hafnium_custom_symbol_type = {
	type = country
	random_valid = no #Choses the first valid loc from top to bottom

		fallback = yes # If nothing else triggers, it will default to this, ignoring triggers.

			OR = {
				has_game_rule = mendelejew_historical_element_only_names_rule
				has_global_variable = custom_element_72_hafnium_global_var
			}
		}
		localization_key = element_hf
